< review>
I'm a big fan of frozen yogurt and this place is now one of my favorites.

The flavors were a pretty standard fare with a few neat options like Acai Berry and Peanut Butter Cup.  The toppings are where this place shined.  They had some pretty unique toppings that I haven't seen at places like Yogurtland and Cherry On Top, two other popular choices for my family, and the toppings just seemed fresher? The staff was nice and the place was pretty clean, sans a slight froyo spill around one of the dispensers.

We'll definitely come back.<//review>

< Review>
Supe cute small cafe and nice enough staff, but not a place to eat beyond pasties or quick grab. They have a full menu available with breakfast all day. We got a cake, waffle and an omelet. The wait was about a half hour for everything but the cake we got right away. It sank my heart to do to do it to a fellow BOH,  but sent the omelet back because it was so overcooked and dry. The cook rolled his eyes then sent out the exact same overcooked brown egg again and topped it with the cheese (not inside at all). The manager checked in later asked if it was better. I told him it wasn't and they just shrugged it off as if not wanting tough overcooked egg omelet is a just a rare preference. No offer to amend the situation of getting something else or making again.
The warm lava cake and waffle were good. The waffle is definitely from a mix, but that's expected in a touristy place.< /Review>

Dr. Arrobio has been our family dentist for more than 25 years. He's been wonderful and we wouldn't see anyone else if not for his recent retirement. He's gentle, matter-of-fact, has a hilarious dry sense of humor and treats his patients with the utmost respect.

< Text>
I've driven by this place so many times.  Finally stopped in after seeing reviews and photos. The food lives up to the hype.  It was delicious!  The chips were fresh and crunchy. The salsa was fresh as well.I had a combo with 2 al pastor tacos & a chicken enchilada. Al pastor flavorful and just the right amount of spicy. The enchilada was good but wasn't as good as the tacos. Don't get me wrong it was good but I liked the other items more.  The rice & beans were tasty. The rice was cooked perfectly, not hard or overcooked and flavored just right not salty. The refried beans were tasty and didn't feel heavy. Can't wait to go back and try more items.

UPDATE - 2/4/2020
I have been here a few more times.  One time I switched it up and tried the al pastor Super Burrito with beans rice guacamole & sour cream.  It was good especially because of the guacamole but there is something about that taco enchilada combo that draws me back to it.  Just know if you go here everything is good you just might find your favorite.</Text>

<rate>5< /rate>< text>
Great food! Really hit the spot. A good amount of food for a great price.

My daughter and I were looking for some great carne asada nearby and chose El Amigo based on the reviews.

We loved the variety of the menu. I had the carne asada plate and my daughter had the carne asada tacos plate. I had the large Tamarindo...the cups are big, but good.

The service at the register was great. They offer complimentary chips and salsa while you wait. True chips and the salsa was perfect. Chunky and bien picante!

The plates came out full to the brim. Table service was great. The steak was seasoned just right and came with grilled onions. The rice and beans were a great compliment, not too dry or too runny.

We finished the plates and ordered some to go for the rest of the family. We will be back!</text>

<text>Such a hidden gem here in the South Bay area. Parking is super limited but we live nearby so we just go walking over. My favorite has to be the tacos here. They are pretty big for a standard taco. The Lengua and Asada are the go to's. Plates are really well served and the location has gotten some major updates in recent years. My lady likes ordering the chile relleno, pretty bomb. I recommend ordering ahead as it can get pretty busy here. The staff is really cool as well. Just know what you want.< /text></record></dataset><record>

< review>
I came here after leaving LAX. It had decent reviews and was close to the freeway. It's small, but had a small lot for parking. There's seating inside and in a covered patio with TVs. I got Ricardo's Super Burrito (dry) with al pastor. Wet probably would have been really good too, something to try next time. The mix of ingredients was balanced and the house salsa was a nice addition. It came with a serrano chile too. Freshly fried chips and salsa were provided. The chips were very light and crunchy, I loved them. Overall, great spot.</review>
